# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="430fe-102">Membri obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="430fe-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="430fe-103">Questo articolo elenca i membri dei tipi obsoleti in .NET Framework 4,5 e versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="430fe-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="430fe-104">I membri dei tipi sono raggruppati per assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="430fe-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="430fe-105">In questo articolo non sono elencati i membri dei tipi obsoleti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="430fe-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="430fe-106">Per un elenco di tipi obsoleti, vedere [tipi obsoleti](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="430fe-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
